<span key="d589f71d056646839ea2cbdb1eb2557b"><span offset-key="d589f71d056646839ea2cbdb1eb2557b:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://codepen.io/gaearon/embed/ozqNOV?editors=0010" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="f66fbd26e8444532a9119abf8cd6eaf3" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="0ffba8cba36546d3bae5221322b65343"><strong>Try it on CodePen</strong></span></span></a><span key="1b4dc66f80ec41a6ac5136d4b99c8d65"><span offset-key="1b4dc66f80ec41a6ac5136d4b99c8d65:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="6fe783f938ab47849a14de173a4d7aa2"><span offset-key="6fe783f938ab47849a14de173a4d7aa2:0">Anything inside the &lt;FancyBorder> JSX tag gets passed into the FancyBorder component as a children prop. Since FancyBorder renders {props.children} inside a &lt;div>, the passed elements appear in the final output.</span></span>

<span key="8c1f9043d8ee443bb8bcaf6269be16a4"><span offset-key="8c1f9043d8ee443bb8bcaf6269be16a4:0">While this is less common, sometimes you might need multiple "holes" in a component. In such cases you may come up with your own convention instead of using children:</span></span>

<span key="713bab6eb52a4265aa0c3aae55f22b43"><span offset-key="713bab6eb52a4265aa0c3aae55f22b43:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://codepen.io/gaearon/embed/gwZOJp?editors=0010" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="c8225d91b5f64c449c48e15dfce52598" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="0f582e5b1912461f93decfd382bd3c49"><strong>Try it on CodePen</strong></span></span></a><span key="4bd2929ce2b5447db73e21566684b276"><span offset-key="4bd2929ce2b5447db73e21566684b276:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="8f92fde380ba4a6f8a66a086e8d28a6a"><span offset-key="8f92fde380ba4a6f8a66a086e8d28a6a:0">React elements like &lt;Contacts /> and &lt;Chat /> are just objects, so you can pass them as props like any other data. This approach may remind you of "slots" in other libraries but there are no limitations on what you can pass as props in React.</span></span>

# 

<span key="1401fd59af3f43da91eac0d1aa56848d"><span offset-key="1401fd59af3f43da91eac0d1aa56848d:0">Specialization</span></span>

<span key="64a558c83a5b4ccfabff3739c467be37"><span offset-key="64a558c83a5b4ccfabff3739c467be37:0">Sometimes we think about components as being "special cases" of other components. For example, we might say that a WelcomeDialog is a special case of Dialog.</span></span>

<span key="dfcb4155cb52450bbdaf0d2b428e246e"><span offset-key="dfcb4155cb52450bbdaf0d2b428e246e:0">In React, this is also achieved by composition, where a more "specific" component renders a more "generic" one and configures it with props:</span></span>

<span key="c329f52e18d44b839dbfb788a560c2fb"><span offset-key="c329f52e18d44b839dbfb788a560c2fb:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://codepen.io/gaearon/embed/kkEaOZ?editors=0010" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="4b370914ecfc41e2a742d7e2b30efdfa" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="b605dce152c54038922704f006f8c976"><strong>Try it on CodePen</strong></span></span></a><span key="1f41cc13074d4e2fbb7268cada32943b"><span offset-key="1f41cc13074d4e2fbb7268cada32943b:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="a17e725830314736bd8743ed761386a7"><span offset-key="a17e725830314736bd8743ed761386a7:0">Composition works equally well for components defined as classes:</span></span>

<span key="7b0b4fd967de4084832d61ea16d534ab"><span offset-key="7b0b4fd967de4084832d61ea16d534ab:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://codepen.io/gaearon/embed/gwZbYa?editors=0010" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="9f479bbc71af48f0ba0141ead404b182" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="2abb69b11c954d29ad7c23f4fa1e6a83"><strong>Try it on CodePen</strong></span></span></a><span key="59ab093ee1a040f198f2fd7676c399ff"><span offset-key="59ab093ee1a040f198f2fd7676c399ff:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

# 

<span key="52bc3c8500634dab9208b02dee38952b"><span offset-key="52bc3c8500634dab9208b02dee38952b:0">So What About Inheritance?</span></span>

<span key="e1707943fa5e48899cd8ad3d533c3745"><span offset-key="e1707943fa5e48899cd8ad3d533c3745:0">At Facebook, we use React in thousands of components, and we haven't found any use cases where we would recommend creating component inheritance hierarchies.</span></span>

<span key="9cbf8b9620cd47bda9eaca0f1debab99"><span offset-key="9cbf8b9620cd47bda9eaca0f1debab99:0">Props and composition give you all the flexibility you need to customize a component's look and behavior in an explicit and safe way. Remember that components may accept arbitrary props, including primitive values, React elements, or functions.</span></span>

<span key="2a881bca67ea4824a2e41a355ca203ab"><span offset-key="2a881bca67ea4824a2e41a355ca203ab:0">If you want to reuse non-UI functionality between components, we suggest extracting it into a separate JavaScript module. The components may import it and use that function, object, or a class, without extending it.</span></span>

# 

<span key="0acca36cd35d4b89812015994d3441cb">**Thinking in React**</span>

# 

<span key="4bad6c6316dc4243a9a6b597c4cbc208"><span offset-key="4bad6c6316dc4243a9a6b597c4cbc208:0">React is, in our opinion, the premier way to build big, fast Web apps with JavaScript. It has scaled very well for us at Facebook and Instagram.</span></span>

<span key="9d9fdf05b58d482094d26a10c50f5fa0"><span offset-key="9d9fdf05b58d482094d26a10c50f5fa0:0">One of the many great parts of React is how it makes you think about apps as you build them. In this document, we'll walk you through the thought process of building a searchable product data table using React.</span></span>

# 

<span key="cd86894b4888460da7be8c83a5948b0a"><span offset-key="cd86894b4888460da7be8c83a5948b0a:0">Start With A Mock</span></span>

<span key="119f8722190c48b6be5abe5d6c21afaf"><span offset-key="119f8722190c48b6be5abe5d6c21afaf:0">Imagine that we already have a JSON API and a mock from our designer. The mock looks like this:</span></span>

<span key="b0e9acf871e14171980156bbe90d3c49"><span offset-key="b0e9acf871e14171980156bbe90d3c49:0">Our JSON API returns some data that looks like this:</span></span>

# 

<span key="4e40aed8826e46b69ad03748af2a2d4b"><span offset-key="4e40aed8826e46b69ad03748af2a2d4b:0">Step 1: Break The UI Into A Component Hierarchy</span></span>

<span key="94591b3582354c8fabf683b6b0ebcc80"><span offset-key="94591b3582354c8fabf683b6b0ebcc80:0">The first thing you'll want to do is to draw boxes around every component (and subcomponent) in the mock and give them all names. If you're working with a designer, they may have already done this, so go talk to them! Their Photoshop layer names may end up being the names of your React components!</span></span>

<span key="e2901c1571d942c2bbcdd1c3c0ab8788"><span offset-key="e2901c1571d942c2bbcdd1c3c0ab8788:0">But how do you know what should be its own component? Use the same techniques for deciding if you should create a new function or object. One such technique is the </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Single_responsibility_principle" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="9716c776723547b6a7b468ba41983f4e" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="dea67c8ea67c4d299c5ca43bc2713f48"><span data-offset-key="dea67c8ea67c4d299c5ca43bc2713f48:0">single responsibility principle</span></span></span></a><span key="3471e0892a3d4c71b4979392f09713f6"><span offset-key="3471e0892a3d4c71b4979392f09713f6:0">, that is, a component should ideally only do one thing. If it ends up growing, it should be decomposed into smaller subcomponents.</span></span>

<span key="c617f4ca4c314a798c9ace1701488837"><span offset-key="c617f4ca4c314a798c9ace1701488837:0">Since you're often displaying a JSON data model to a user, you'll find that if your model was built correctly, your UI (and therefore your component structure) will map nicely. That's because UI and data models tend to adhere to the same </span>*information architecture*<span offset-key="c617f4ca4c314a798c9ace1701488837:2">. Separate your UI into components, where each component matches one piece of your data model.</span></span>

<span key="5de5a58a48504b23866e6fca5c8eb6c6"><span offset-key="5de5a58a48504b23866e6fca5c8eb6c6:0">You'll see here that we have five components in our app. We've italicized the data each component represents.</span></span>

1.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">1.</span>
    <span key="9ac24efbb564421682b524a8f7510bf5">**FilterableProductTable (orange):**<span offset-key="9ac24efbb564421682b524a8f7510bf5:1"> contains the entirety of the example</span></span>

2.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">2.</span>
    <span key="57d86bd494d544d390c59e1b912c8e4d">**SearchBar (blue):**<span offset-key="57d86bd494d544d390c59e1b912c8e4d:1"> receives all </span>*user input*</span>

3.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">3.</span>
    <span key="be3c20f218b64b7e913f46eb08ae526f">**ProductTable (green):**<span offset-key="be3c20f218b64b7e913f46eb08ae526f:1"> displays and filters the </span>*data collection*<span offset-key="be3c20f218b64b7e913f46eb08ae526f:3"> based on </span>*user input*</span>

4.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">4.</span>
    <span key="c74e39c809914fe8b6e2adc1ea72c680">**ProductCategoryRow (turquoise):**<span offset-key="c74e39c809914fe8b6e2adc1ea72c680:1"> displays a heading for each </span>*category*</span>

5.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">5.</span>
    <span key="3b8ba2ad5c414b32b37fd33eac6b4ac4">**ProductRow (red):**<span offset-key="3b8ba2ad5c414b32b37fd33eac6b4ac4:1"> displays a row for each </span>*product*</span>

<span key="aca87a7104c246cc9928a7146c58d815"><span offset-key="aca87a7104c246cc9928a7146c58d815:0">If you look at ProductTable, you'll see that the table header (containing the "Name" and "Price" labels) isn't its own component. This is a matter of preference, and there's an argument to be made either way. For this example, we left it as part of ProductTable because it is part of rendering the </span>*data collection*<span offset-key="aca87a7104c246cc9928a7146c58d815:2"> which is ProductTable's responsibility. However, if this header grows to be complex (e.g., if we were to add affordances for sorting), it would certainly make sense to make this its own ProductTableHeader component.</span></span>

<span key="c662e09665dc45c1becefe8fefa49d14"><span offset-key="c662e09665dc45c1becefe8fefa49d14:0">Now that we've identified the components in our mock, let's arrange them into a hierarchy. Components that appear within another component in the mock should appear as a child in the hierarchy:</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="fa4d62eec89848ee875db351b2c9e18a"><span offset-key="fa4d62eec89848ee875db351b2c9e18a:0">FilterableProductTable</span></span>

    -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

        <span key="ca5f580bb7d945569d6b97613279c2e7"><span offset-key="ca5f580bb7d945569d6b97613279c2e7:0">SearchBar</span></span>

    -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

        <span key="4cda905e2c964acba185f6465084f284"><span offset-key="4cda905e2c964acba185f6465084f284:0">ProductTable</span></span>

        -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

            <span key="90c328506e0d49b5a41ba3462b087b3f"><span offset-key="90c328506e0d49b5a41ba3462b087b3f:0">ProductCategoryRow</span></span>

        -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

            <span key="a8a9c709328045ccb217a8601aecf912"><span offset-key="a8a9c709328045ccb217a8601aecf912:0">ProductRow</span></span>

# 

<span key="183dc9d7ad2d4b49b2f41d6e0c6ba514"><span offset-key="183dc9d7ad2d4b49b2f41d6e0c6ba514:0">Step 2: Build A Static Version in React</span></span>

<span key="052ec708c48b42c5a36b75947bd5521c"><span offset-key="052ec708c48b42c5a36b75947bd5521c:0">See the Pen </span></span><a href="https://codepen.io/gaearon/embed/BwWzwm" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="76a9c26bfb634490bd823efa0cf29599" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="86efe52e6b1642448fb78d7fbe30d1a4"><span data-offset-key="86efe52e6b1642448fb78d7fbe30d1a4:0">Thinking In React: Step 2</span></span></span></a><span key="724a840fce884cfbac36163eead828b3"><span offset-key="724a840fce884cfbac36163eead828b3:0"> on </span></span><a href="https://codepen.io" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="76a442bfeb8a4543a7d3c7f949de3aa0" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="ddd3e4e2f988468b88a8c9f79c59beca"><span data-offset-key="ddd3e4e2f988468b88a8c9f79c59beca:0">CodePen</span></span></span></a><span key="6c2706f1dcd644af926da522fb6093be"><span offset-key="6c2706f1dcd644af926da522fb6093be:0">.</span></span>

<span key="22c2f8f21299473b8353f754f2bd1964"><span offset-key="22c2f8f21299473b8353f754f2bd1964:0">Now that you have your component hierarchy, it's time to implement your app. The easiest way is to build a version that takes your data model and renders the UI but has no interactivity. It's best to decouple these processes because building a static version requires a lot of typing and no thinking, and adding interactivity requires a lot of thinking and not a lot of typing. We'll see why.</span></span>

<span key="49167273c0d24012b631ab4db8122b83"><span offset-key="49167273c0d24012b631ab4db8122b83:0">To build a static version of your app that renders your data model, you'll want to build components that reuse other components and pass data using </span>*props*<span offset-key="49167273c0d24012b631ab4db8122b83:2">. </span>*props*<span offset-key="49167273c0d24012b631ab4db8122b83:4"> are a way of passing data from parent to child. If you're familiar with the concept of </span>*state*<span offset-key="49167273c0d24012b631ab4db8122b83:6">, </span>**don't use state at all**<span offset-key="49167273c0d24012b631ab4db8122b83:8"> to build this static version. State is reserved only for interactivity, that is, data that changes over time. Since this is a static version of the app, you don't need it.</span></span>

<span key="d651dd5ba4fb46ba98834f4786b4429e"><span offset-key="d651dd5ba4fb46ba98834f4786b4429e:0">You can build top-down or bottom-up. That is, you can either start with building the components higher up in the hierarchy (i.e. starting with FilterableProductTable) or with the ones lower in it (ProductRow). In simpler examples, it's usually easier to go top-down, and on larger projects, it's easier to go bottom-up and write tests as you build.</span></span>

<span key="c49af311547a41dda418b8d7806ade5f"><span offset-key="c49af311547a41dda418b8d7806ade5f:0">At the end of this step, you'll have a library of reusable components that render your data model. The components will only have render() methods since this is a static version of your app. The component at the top of the hierarchy (FilterableProductTable) will take your data model as a prop. If you make a change to your underlying data model and call ReactDOM.render() again, the UI will be updated. You can see how your UI is updated and where to make changes. React's </span>**one-way data flow**<span offset-key="c49af311547a41dda418b8d7806ade5f:2"> (also called </span>*one-way binding*<span offset-key="c49af311547a41dda418b8d7806ade5f:4">) keeps everything modular and fast.</span></span>

<span key="d9fe2bc0afdd4ac38350de8cbd3d23ae"><span offset-key="d9fe2bc0afdd4ac38350de8cbd3d23ae:0">Refer to the </span></span><a href="https://reactjs.org/docs/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="55659b7f81324cacb09a8133367bc642" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="041e6ca8fb50463d8b3a36a0df2bcee8"><span data-offset-key="041e6ca8fb50463d8b3a36a0df2bcee8:0">React docs</span></span></span></a><span key="57354db04419423382f92890daada2e5"><span offset-key="57354db04419423382f92890daada2e5:0"> if you need help executing this step.</span></span>

# 

<span key="9c35c96e4d3343df9a15bdb125367a1d"><span offset-key="9c35c96e4d3343df9a15bdb125367a1d:0">A Brief Interlude: Props vs State</span></span>

<span key="782e510d00fb4b548a406b9106d82dec"><span offset-key="782e510d00fb4b548a406b9106d82dec:0">There are two types of "model" data in React: props and state. It's important to understand the distinction between the two; skim </span></span><a href="https://reactjs.org/docs/state-and-lifecycle.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="7306e0a8231a433ba909993d5a2b6666" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="74c39046b4a14cb0a6341a64f8c214d2"><span data-offset-key="74c39046b4a14cb0a6341a64f8c214d2:0">the official React docs</span></span></span></a><span key="91b0741d298c45d0bc283bde1882151c"><span offset-key="91b0741d298c45d0bc283bde1882151c:0"> if you aren't sure what the difference is. See also </span></span><a href="https://reactjs.org/docs/faq-state.html#what-is-the-difference-between-state-and-props" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="7efa1818e9584b5b8b2c829a3c345961" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="2b6b7bbccf1b407a80aa720ab617846c"><span data-offset-key="2b6b7bbccf1b407a80aa720ab617846c:0">FAQ: What is the difference between state and props?</span></span></span></a><span key="5a6d6e2b719849c396042dfb8861a0d1"><span offset-key="5a6d6e2b719849c396042dfb8861a0d1:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

# 

<span key="716ee007c2984af59ea8ececb42cb8b0"><span offset-key="716ee007c2984af59ea8ececb42cb8b0:0">Step 3: Identify The Minimal (but complete) Representation Of UI State</span></span>

<span key="95a460ac480f4af2925906979f77c819"><span offset-key="95a460ac480f4af2925906979f77c819:0">To make your UI interactive, you need to be able to trigger changes to your underlying data model. React achieves this with </span>**state**<span offset-key="95a460ac480f4af2925906979f77c819:2">.</span></span>

<span key="52c1fbb60614466baaff73940e0c831c"><span offset-key="52c1fbb60614466baaff73940e0c831c:0">To build your app correctly, you first need to think of the minimal set of mutable state that your app needs. The key here is </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Don&#39;t_repeat_yourself" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="c6f6e63d7fe24d569204f6ad50b95269" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="6659a2dd649640059304e55be1a14356"><span data-offset-key="6659a2dd649640059304e55be1a14356:0">DRY: </span><em>Don't Repeat Yourself</em></span></span></a><span key="2208979450e04988946482b3c0f2b467"><span offset-key="2208979450e04988946482b3c0f2b467:0">. Figure out the absolute minimal representation of the state your application needs and compute everything else you need on-demand. For example, if you're building a TODO list, keep an array of the TODO items around; don't keep a separate state variable for the count. Instead, when you want to render the TODO count, take the length of the TODO items array.</span></span>

<span key="14c7f152a2cf4e05a57588411df5dc3c"><span offset-key="14c7f152a2cf4e05a57588411df5dc3c:0">Think of all the pieces of data in our example application. We have:</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="8b903ef4a2574ff794897cc179a9b743"><span offset-key="8b903ef4a2574ff794897cc179a9b743:0">The original list of products</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="22cd23dfda0e4f34a3efa8ec9e58fa6f"><span offset-key="22cd23dfda0e4f34a3efa8ec9e58fa6f:0">The search text the user has entered</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="d419529ce5094ca2b994b0633e899cca"><span offset-key="d419529ce5094ca2b994b0633e899cca:0">The value of the checkbox</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="220aba9eb2a94778852f98d1cbcb9a83"><span offset-key="220aba9eb2a94778852f98d1cbcb9a83:0">The filtered list of products</span></span>

<span key="d33d1aeefd8344f8a5da92358eecf87b"><span offset-key="d33d1aeefd8344f8a5da92358eecf87b:0">Let's go through each one and figure out which one is state. Ask three questions about each piece of data:</span></span>

1.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">1.</span>
    <span key="ee8f1f01f4044d7f9f2db01aa04b67b8"><span offset-key="ee8f1f01f4044d7f9f2db01aa04b67b8:0">Is it passed in from a parent via props? If so, it probably isn't state.</span></span>

2.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">2.</span>
    <span key="8a692343f9bc41c7a0674d3c3c48807e"><span offset-key="8a692343f9bc41c7a0674d3c3c48807e:0">Does it remain unchanged over time? If so, it probably isn't state.</span></span>

3.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">3.</span>
    <span key="efd2daa86fc543fd88901b364e138874"><span offset-key="efd2daa86fc543fd88901b364e138874:0">Can you compute it based on any other state or props in your component? If so, it isn't state.</span></span>

<span key="3fca0e4b431042d3bc4ce292121a7feb"><span offset-key="3fca0e4b431042d3bc4ce292121a7feb:0">The original list of products is passed in as props, so that's not state. The search text and the checkbox seem to be state since they change over time and can't be computed from anything. And finally, the filtered list of products isn't state because it can be computed by combining the original list of products with the search text and value of the checkbox.</span></span>

<span key="a0de8c6fa16a4d20b2157ab28148a3b3"><span offset-key="a0de8c6fa16a4d20b2157ab28148a3b3:0">So finally, our state is:</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="c0d6b5d8c10b4f1c894b0e8f96528657"><span offset-key="c0d6b5d8c10b4f1c894b0e8f96528657:0">The search text the user has entered</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="fcc9e0ca950644618f6cfa28c843dc1b"><span offset-key="fcc9e0ca950644618f6cfa28c843dc1b:0">The value of the checkbox</span></span>

# 

<span key="6fe179a4159b4754bd32e2574f128917"><span offset-key="6fe179a4159b4754bd32e2574f128917:0">Step 4: Identify Where Your State Should Live</span></span>

<span key="655c4f562f71429299ef4c0de0a6b1f3"><span offset-key="655c4f562f71429299ef4c0de0a6b1f3:0">See the Pen </span></span><a href="https://codepen.io/gaearon/embed/qPrNQZ" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="b33da810ffeb40f59eb4723f146dbe96" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="a2c1f307880a41d7a10ca19d3f27df22"><span data-offset-key="a2c1f307880a41d7a10ca19d3f27df22:0">Thinking In React: Step 4</span></span></span></a><span key="9f5d355d2b9849a2a5f9fdc30152245a"><span offset-key="9f5d355d2b9849a2a5f9fdc30152245a:0"> on </span></span><a href="https://codepen.io" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="c4896e9fa9054578957f5aab97fcb7e1" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="f55294fa7ac5454997afd766dbe6810d"><span data-offset-key="f55294fa7ac5454997afd766dbe6810d:0">CodePen</span></span></span></a><span key="0dbe9b4da3fa410c82623a8bd3e6e898"><span offset-key="0dbe9b4da3fa410c82623a8bd3e6e898:0">.</span></span>

<span key="675a239afa6e4501a0f72c7b5fdf4860"><span offset-key="675a239afa6e4501a0f72c7b5fdf4860:0">OK, so we've identified what the minimal set of app state is. Next, we need to identify which component mutates, or </span>*owns*<span offset-key="675a239afa6e4501a0f72c7b5fdf4860:2">, this state.</span></span>

<span key="14f3c49602fa4bcf8ca2d5a7a6813955"><span offset-key="14f3c49602fa4bcf8ca2d5a7a6813955:0">Remember: React is all about one-way data flow down the component hierarchy. It may not be immediately clear which component should own what state. </span>**This is often the most challenging part for newcomers to understand,**<span offset-key="14f3c49602fa4bcf8ca2d5a7a6813955:2"> so follow these steps to figure it out:</span></span>

<span key="ef7ca0b7e02d4b7298141a0a7058e51a"><span offset-key="ef7ca0b7e02d4b7298141a0a7058e51a:0">For each piece of state in your application:</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="a9fdc65fe1c74bd0b933d68f5e9aefdf"><span offset-key="a9fdc65fe1c74bd0b933d68f5e9aefdf:0">Identify every component that renders something based on that state.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="22ee594a915e4c889602a48efb9e8138"><span offset-key="22ee594a915e4c889602a48efb9e8138:0">Find a common owner component (a single component above all the components that need the state in the hierarchy).</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="89fd4a59a37a45e78ab81672ce22b139"><span offset-key="89fd4a59a37a45e78ab81672ce22b139:0">Either the common owner or another component higher up in the hierarchy should own the state.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="43895abc588b41e7907424398b276670"><span offset-key="43895abc588b41e7907424398b276670:0">If you can't find a component where it makes sense to own the state, create a new component solely for holding the state and add it somewhere in the hierarchy above the common owner component.</span></span>

<span key="331b9ebf648c418daf83ba37816a6d1e"><span offset-key="331b9ebf648c418daf83ba37816a6d1e:0">Let's run through this strategy for our application:</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="4fab204bc9244b20bd218c8a88ef1640"><span offset-key="4fab204bc9244b20bd218c8a88ef1640:0">ProductTable needs to filter the product list based on state and SearchBar needs to display the search text and checked state.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="171a35e7b0af4dcf95b7f1692241a781"><span offset-key="171a35e7b0af4dcf95b7f1692241a781:0">The common owner component is FilterableProductTable.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="f656e18f18d8463e9fb14f08f05f5168"><span offset-key="f656e18f18d8463e9fb14f08f05f5168:0">It conceptually makes sense for the filter text and checked value to live in FilterableProductTable</span></span>

<span key="230cff2c6f8a4c9b84a34478b90eff9b"><span offset-key="230cff2c6f8a4c9b84a34478b90eff9b:0">Cool, so we've decided that our state lives in FilterableProductTable. First, add an instance property this.state = {filterText: '', inStockOnly: false} to FilterableProductTable's constructor to reflect the initial state of your application. Then, pass filterText and inStockOnly to ProductTable and SearchBar as a prop. Finally, use these props to filter the rows in ProductTable and set the values of the form fields in SearchBar.</span></span>

<span key="1e10b6824c00409b938667ffe57769f0"><span offset-key="1e10b6824c00409b938667ffe57769f0:0">You can start seeing how your application will behave: set filterText to "ball" and refresh your app. You'll see that the data table is updated correctly.</span></span>

# 

<span key="0f3b1714fba14a619032ba5da76aacb0"><span offset-key="0f3b1714fba14a619032ba5da76aacb0:0">Step 5: Add Inverse Data Flow</span></span>

<span key="77183f508c5b4f16baa623eb0c1bf649"><span offset-key="77183f508c5b4f16baa623eb0c1bf649:0">See the Pen </span></span><a href="https://codepen.io/gaearon/embed/LzWZvb" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="4cc1f48109b045818980acdbb35c2a42" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="edbe907dd03c4cd0ba71ea923df05fc3"><span data-offset-key="edbe907dd03c4cd0ba71ea923df05fc3:0">Thinking In React: Step 5</span></span></span></a><span key="bdabfb3970df4f9b9e7a7502f64f8a30"><span offset-key="bdabfb3970df4f9b9e7a7502f64f8a30:0"> on </span></span><a href="https://codepen.io" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="e464487d5b15475b9a775d28c82fd5b6" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="e286b2443d854525ae3eb684561ffa9b"><span data-offset-key="e286b2443d854525ae3eb684561ffa9b:0">CodePen</span></span></span></a><span key="efe8933275214810bcc2e8cdb004c063"><span offset-key="efe8933275214810bcc2e8cdb004c063:0">.</span></span>

<span key="5eaac777d41a4ba2891e842feda1a404"><span offset-key="5eaac777d41a4ba2891e842feda1a404:0">So far, we've built an app that renders correctly as a function of props and state flowing down the hierarchy. Now it's time to support data flowing the other way: the form components deep in the hierarchy need to update the state in FilterableProductTable.</span></span>

<span key="c028996373254a2a99ea2ffcbfaa2d78"><span offset-key="c028996373254a2a99ea2ffcbfaa2d78:0">React makes this data flow explicit to help you understand how your program works, but it does require a little more typing than traditional two-way data binding.</span></span>

<span key="5ca75587739a4e88b905137291df49f4"><span offset-key="5ca75587739a4e88b905137291df49f4:0">If you try to type or check the box in the current version of the example, you'll see that React ignores your input. This is intentional, as we've set the value prop of the input to always be equal to the state passed in from FilterableProductTable.</span></span>

<span key="1e07cabf7de241b98e34aac31271da95"><span offset-key="1e07cabf7de241b98e34aac31271da95:0">Let's think about what we want to happen. We want to make sure that whenever the user changes the form, we update the state to reflect the user input. Since components should only update their own state, FilterableProductTable will pass callbacks to SearchBar that will fire whenever the state should be updated. We can use the onChange event on the inputs to be notified of it. The callbacks passed by FilterableProductTable will call setState(), and the app will be updated.</span></span>

# 

<span key="f30847d6f6a64bf3ad3d40f525a3f019"><span offset-key="f30847d6f6a64bf3ad3d40f525a3f019:0">And That's It</span></span>

<span key="ac21a4c4714f47c38d7d395646bc9cd1"><span offset-key="ac21a4c4714f47c38d7d395646bc9cd1:0">Hopefully, this gives you an idea of how to think about building components and applications with React. While it may be a little more typing than you're used to, remember that code is read far more than it's written, and it's less difficult to read this modular, explicit code. As you start to build large libraries of components, you'll appreciate this explicitness and modularity, and with code reuse, your lines of code will start to shrink. :)</span></span>

<span key="d0d59bc749784cbd99fd7d0dfd05ea10"><span offset-key="d0d59bc749784cbd99fd7d0dfd05ea10:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.notion.so/Advanced-Content-fbe1ec3ca3544951b5763b051b843949" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="31f23d81b1f54a08a5ab0dfd658bb6b8" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="92a884ab0452489fa11d21171589bcf1"><span data-offset-key="92a884ab0452489fa11d21171589bcf1:0">Advanced Content</span></span></span></a><span key="7b84d9b1d968450db977e8c5fcaa1042"><span offset-key="7b84d9b1d968450db977e8c5fcaa1042:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="92140839d39046cea75019ba3645fd33"><span offset-key="92140839d39046cea75019ba3645fd33:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.notion.so/React-Component-3dc17bc49a8e4d7e89efcc1281e747d9" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="35055fbee30742cea464411bbae50800" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="bfcc87ead76e428698e395f1aa061bdd"><span data-offset-key="bfcc87ead76e428698e395f1aa061bdd:0">React Component</span></span></span></a><span key="b142f192507546a8ada535f43dd5fbdf"><span offset-key="b142f192507546a8ada535f43dd5fbdf:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

# 

<span key="2b75888ef2d64bbe874e81a1616c4c32"><span offset-key="2b75888ef2d64bbe874e81a1616c4c32:0">Getting Startednpx create-react-app my-appcd my-appnpm startnpx create-react-app my-appnpm init react-app my-appyarn create react-app my-appnpx create-react-app my-app --template \[template-name\]npx create-react-app my-app --template typescriptnpx create-react-app my-app --use-npmmy-appâ”œâ”€â”€ README.mdâ”œâ”€â”€ node\_modulesâ”œâ”€â”€ package.jsonâ”œâ”€â”€ .gitignoreâ”œâ”€â”€ publicâ”‚ â”œâ”€â”€ favicon.icoâ”‚ â”œâ”€â”€ index.htmlâ”‚ â”œâ”€â”€ logo192.pngâ”‚ â”œâ”€â”€ logo512.pngâ”‚ â”œâ”€â”€ manifest.jsonâ”‚ â””â”€â”€ robots.txtâ””â”€â”€ src â”œâ”€â”€ App.css â”œâ”€â”€ App.js â”œâ”€â”€ App.test.js â”œâ”€â”€ index.css â”œâ”€â”€ index.js â”œâ”€â”€ logo.svg â”œâ”€â”€ serviceWorker.js â””â”€â”€ setupTests.jscd my-app</span></span>

<span key="b16bfb9cb93b40cea0bfcccfb4559fc4"><span offset-key="b16bfb9cb93b40cea0bfcccfb4559fc4:0">Create React App is an officially supported way to create single-page React applications. It offers a modern build setup with no configuration.</span></span>

## 

<span key="56f5bad594de454fb9ec3be1a1bd0964"><span offset-key="56f5bad594de454fb9ec3be1a1bd0964:0">Quick Start</span></span><a href="https://create-react-app.dev/docs/getting-started#quick-start" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="6267ca2c55cc4aeabdfc27ef05316c1b" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="b319a37f811842519a34c1f9c5a3cedf"><span data-offset-key="b319a37f811842519a34c1f9c5a3cedf:0">#</span></span></span></a><span key="426cfda7338242e9993b2ad3e26119b8"><span offset-key="426cfda7338242e9993b2ad3e26119b8:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

> <span key="256dc45cd3d74c3dba741d65c8decb09"><span offset-key="256dc45cd3d74c3dba741d65c8decb09:0">If you've previously installed create-react-app globally via npm install -g create-react-app, we recommend you uninstall the package using npm uninstall -g create-react-app or yarn global remove create-react-app to ensure that npx always uses the latest version.</span></span>

<span key="915ee5714a774a4e9d161ecf93de2ea4">*(*</span><a href="https://medium.com/@maybekatz/introducing-npx-an-npm-package-runner-55f7d4bd282b" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="e97bb682486d46f591f254b056c2866d" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="c3fce0f2bf944c01b3d1296107e835d6"><em>npx</em></span></span></a><span key="c232eac6221840aba148bacdf7bc3803"><span offset-key="c232eac6221840aba148bacdf7bc3803:0">\* comes with npm 5.2+ and higher, see </span></span><a href="https://gist.github.com/gaearon/4064d3c23a77c74a3614c498a8bb1c5f" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="b86e829736024787be414fd9c8ad8a96" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="d4b4bbece20a4fdfa9681edca2982351"><em>instructions for older npm versions</em></span></span></a><span key="94c9fd7b9d964abbb99ab2700fc8eb60"><span offset-key="94c9fd7b9d964abbb99ab2700fc8eb60:0">)\*</span></span>

<span key="67804b39661f4b06976d13b5f9a1ebee"><span offset-key="67804b39661f4b06976d13b5f9a1ebee:0">Then open </span></span><a href="http://localhost:3000" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="895be5de0ee443d5a622c168bacca3db" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="ef8e1d6cdded4a9fb549dbdb70cec60c"><span data-offset-key="ef8e1d6cdded4a9fb549dbdb70cec60c:0">http://localhost:3000/</span></span></span></a><span key="55b33512e50049e29d3431ef88ebf0d5"><span offset-key="55b33512e50049e29d3431ef88ebf0d5:0"> to see your app.</span></span>

<span key="130b09c105f74695b379aa51c085e0e3"><span offset-key="130b09c105f74695b379aa51c085e0e3:0">When youâ€™re ready to deploy to production, create a minified bundle with npm run build.</span></span>

### 

<span key="a040b1bddcba452ea19bd56578ecc43a"><span offset-key="a040b1bddcba452ea19bd56578ecc43a:0">Get Started Immediately</span></span><a href="https://create-react-app.dev/docs/getting-started#get-started-immediately" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="a163fb4d76bf426ebb856c20b12fe466" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="e84a102b35494bafa0e37910941c99b0"><span data-offset-key="e84a102b35494bafa0e37910941c99b0:0">#</span></span></span></a><span key="534c03207e8d4f59addc77b9fbdd6411"><span offset-key="534c03207e8d4f59addc77b9fbdd6411:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="6cacd5c8f58242efb72b05e4e5948525"><span offset-key="6cacd5c8f58242efb72b05e4e5948525:0">You </span>**donâ€™t**<span offset-key="6cacd5c8f58242efb72b05e4e5948525:2"> need to install or configure tools like webpack or Babel. They are preconfigured and hidden so that you can focus on the code.</span></span>

<span key="f12ce694b2ce4998875e75a8af5e5a67"><span offset-key="f12ce694b2ce4998875e75a8af5e5a67:0">Create a project, and youâ€™re good to go.</span></span>

## 

<span key="55799cf0dc9844c388b1a882002ab280"><span offset-key="55799cf0dc9844c388b1a882002ab280:0">Creating an App</span></span><a href="https://create-react-app.dev/docs/getting-started#creating-an-app" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="5ed00ca9b2fb479ab92cf1e1ed3849ff" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="56e42aaa209c4d5382596f31e2575480"><span data-offset-key="56e42aaa209c4d5382596f31e2575480:0">#</span></span></span></a><span key="3f21a5d146364ce5b84839235fb5eb0b"><span offset-key="3f21a5d146364ce5b84839235fb5eb0b:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="06fa8557fec54208ab886c7016326c85">**Youâ€™ll need to have Node &gt;= 10 on your local development machine**<span offset-key="06fa8557fec54208ab886c7016326c85:1"> (but itâ€™s not required on the server). You can use </span></span><a href="https://github.com/creationix/nvm#installation" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="3a87a2d2b98b4c0b93391d154e24fe13" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="06fee6e4a0a0426a9c777b1c5689a103"><span data-offset-key="06fee6e4a0a0426a9c777b1c5689a103:0">nvm</span></span></span></a><span key="cea662666e574b04a51da0d4d12b430a"><span offset-key="cea662666e574b04a51da0d4d12b430a:0"> (macOS/Linux) or </span></span><a href="https://github.com/coreybutler/nvm-windows#node-version-manager-nvm-for-windows" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="c53205002add469d96351362f156937e" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="4cdc23b2ef9b4d888c640ae47dac0013"><span data-offset-key="4cdc23b2ef9b4d888c640ae47dac0013:0">nvm-windows</span></span></span></a><span key="27e7002f78ab42d2a2a141d455b906f4"><span offset-key="27e7002f78ab42d2a2a141d455b906f4:0"> to switch Node versions between different projects.</span></span>

<span key="d62d3ba844654df9b99099596dbf154e"><span offset-key="d62d3ba844654df9b99099596dbf154e:0">To create a new app, you may choose one of the following methods:</span></span>

### 

<span key="a5160f75dc3541c899a90db628cc7cc2"><span offset-key="a5160f75dc3541c899a90db628cc7cc2:0">npx</span></span><a href="https://create-react-app.dev/docs/getting-started#npx" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="007735d68da843638d1fcb816399f30d" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="eac2b47a2fd64c50a3fb94830f92edea"><span data-offset-key="eac2b47a2fd64c50a3fb94830f92edea:0">#</span></span></span></a><span key="4cc1df51d7dd4b579ab2d56545597c21"><span offset-key="4cc1df51d7dd4b579ab2d56545597c21:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="fe50e33f2ef54ca79a11c9ddaa5d83ff">*(*</span><a href="https://medium.com/@maybekatz/introducing-npx-an-npm-package-runner-55f7d4bd282b" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="18b47a3d121041b88d674820fd20bbeb" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="d6147eb453a84281b589fe7d31b9ae2e"><em>npx</em></span></span></a><span key="965805bb1ec34415af3cf5b4a4682ac4"><span offset-key="965805bb1ec34415af3cf5b4a4682ac4:0">\* comes with npm 5.2+ and higher, see </span></span><a href="https://gist.github.com/gaearon/4064d3c23a77c74a3614c498a8bb1c5f" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="157e83388cc5473cbbea394bed6c8ac6" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="f3d3412f47a64a6fa94e66e5478de63a"><em>instructions for older npm versions</em></span></span></a><span key="1193475fb50041c9842ef9ffefd6ba40"><span offset-key="1193475fb50041c9842ef9ffefd6ba40:0">)\*</span></span>

### 

<span key="6729c1e8642e4bec8e909fda0b1c680a"><span offset-key="6729c1e8642e4bec8e909fda0b1c680a:0">npm</span></span><a href="https://create-react-app.dev/docs/getting-started#npm" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="ca627974411f412f991390790fa8bd35" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="9c06ec83b5b94424ac855f96c310cfac"><span data-offset-key="9c06ec83b5b94424ac855f96c310cfac:0">#</span></span></span></a><span key="3fda357a98054029b587c567aaca91bd"><span offset-key="3fda357a98054029b587c567aaca91bd:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

### 

<span key="a90f97b5b9424bf6bee70716bf2fd014"><span offset-key="a90f97b5b9424bf6bee70716bf2fd014:0">Yarn</span></span><a href="https://create-react-app.dev/docs/getting-started#yarn" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="f5ae2a29c8e949e38be46b37ea680a67" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="d11bb246b19043058fecacc8a8e45a87"><span data-offset-key="d11bb246b19043058fecacc8a8e45a87:0">#</span></span></span></a><span key="b54b1f300a394018aa4ff3c756336bc9"><span offset-key="b54b1f300a394018aa4ff3c756336bc9:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="35517e85d1804f9c967a6c5133b330ea">*yarn create is available in Yarn 0.25+*</span>

### 

<span key="6ed772e903f2451a83dd2ca98eb988d4"><span offset-key="6ed772e903f2451a83dd2ca98eb988d4:0">Selecting a template</span></span><a href="https://create-react-app.dev/docs/getting-started#selecting-a-template" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="1b089db6ca2e4b8ea45345da45154952" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="ff96c9c480d64800a59e965241b6c56e"><span data-offset-key="ff96c9c480d64800a59e965241b6c56e:0">#</span></span></span></a><span key="0aff9e0de708429985eacbce59abf95b"><span offset-key="0aff9e0de708429985eacbce59abf95b:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="86dc64fec2da485aa87092302d85948d"><span offset-key="86dc64fec2da485aa87092302d85948d:0">You can now optionally start a new app from a template by appending --template \[template-name\] to the creation command.</span></span>

<span key="5ac9b6cb86b4436497b4ccd70cf99340"><span offset-key="5ac9b6cb86b4436497b4ccd70cf99340:0">If you don't select a template, we'll create your project with our base template.</span></span>

<span key="15490be2f8a44fbe8ed1d3f06bd6eb0e"><span offset-key="15490be2f8a44fbe8ed1d3f06bd6eb0e:0">Templates are always named in the format cra-template-\[template-name\], however you only need to provide the \[template-name\] to the creation command.</span></span>

> <span key="4af5ed8bd1024d468a5b1ad5bb84e8d7"><span offset-key="4af5ed8bd1024d468a5b1ad5bb84e8d7:0">You can find a list of available templates by searching for </span></span><a href="https://www.npmjs.com/search?q=cra-template-*" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="cb57fc3af9c7423594148039e9681097" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="232914e847e142af891d0c2a1f1729eb"><span data-offset-key="232914e847e142af891d0c2a1f1729eb:0">"cra-template-*"</span></span></span></a><span key="2a7e835f08e24d5599775645cb30c61c"><span offset-key="2a7e835f08e24d5599775645cb30c61c:0"> on npm.</span></span>

<span key="986a2fba2b5540d9985a9246ee6e2f3c"><span offset-key="986a2fba2b5540d9985a9246ee6e2f3c:0">Our </span></span><a href="https://create-react-app.dev/docs/custom-templates" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="b153b317ae7a4e668a8ee14f2ecac5db" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="cfe11fab59404ed6a0babc940d984ed5"><span data-offset-key="cfe11fab59404ed6a0babc940d984ed5:0">Custom Templates</span></span></span></a><span key="2e175852470545f8b3311c413b3a3354"><span offset-key="2e175852470545f8b3311c413b3a3354:0"> documentation describes how you can build your own template.</span></span>

<span key="9ce2e1b0c793400fb13ce52ad6a943c9">**Creating a TypeScript app#**</span>

<span key="7e53020a27df4beca0edc6c83c504f68"><span offset-key="7e53020a27df4beca0edc6c83c504f68:0">You can start a new TypeScript app using templates. To use our provided TypeScript template, append --template typescript to the creation command.</span></span>

<span key="0efb0a9c71fd4a5fbe2fd4377d1080d5"><span offset-key="0efb0a9c71fd4a5fbe2fd4377d1080d5:0">If you already have a project and would like to add TypeScript, see our </span></span><a href="https://create-react-app.dev/docs/adding-typescript" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="cf61ae7c62a84424ae5fa9117a956d4c" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="7044c87acfdd4df7a9c0ea3e3db4552e"><span data-offset-key="7044c87acfdd4df7a9c0ea3e3db4552e:0">Adding TypeScript</span></span></span></a><span key="b898b1e0b5164f4b9db52bcba2c50b1e"><span offset-key="b898b1e0b5164f4b9db52bcba2c50b1e:0"> documentation.</span></span>

### 

<span key="d724fc35e9224f398791d16eb534ab09"><span offset-key="d724fc35e9224f398791d16eb534ab09:0">Selecting a package manager</span></span><a href="https://create-react-app.dev/docs/getting-started#selecting-a-package-manager" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="6ee37c34ed8d4b639b886e358edb6152" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="ee0df5327bee40cd85c4d2cbf3a08ab5"><span data-offset-key="ee0df5327bee40cd85c4d2cbf3a08ab5:0">#</span></span></span></a><span key="d8916228dcef4f758eb1bddc7ffef8fe"><span offset-key="d8916228dcef4f758eb1bddc7ffef8fe:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="5f2a2e1af02d418196534d5756863406"><span offset-key="5f2a2e1af02d418196534d5756863406:0">When you create a new app, the CLI will use </span></span><a href="https://yarnpkg.com" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="7e6c22dd678e42f9a982c8b0826ec9e3" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="1b7d43d4b63641a0907f7514dff7439c"><span data-offset-key="1b7d43d4b63641a0907f7514dff7439c:0">Yarn</span></span></span></a><span key="39ff7f721ab24df49f9dfdf3a7a33555"><span offset-key="39ff7f721ab24df49f9dfdf3a7a33555:0"> to install dependencies (when available). If you have Yarn installed, but would prefer to use npm, you can append --use-npm to the creation command. For example:</span></span>

## 

<span key="4a2d8149f6d04a2e83f97ff5519b4e71"><span offset-key="4a2d8149f6d04a2e83f97ff5519b4e71:0">Output</span></span><a href="https://create-react-app.dev/docs/getting-started#output" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="ba495dd4494344bba781d43a9e5402b6" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="8fb096c377794940a711fee0f6cfdf04"><span data-offset-key="8fb096c377794940a711fee0f6cfdf04:0">#</span></span></span></a><span key="2525317e6f8b41509f0b08b99a681a4c"><span offset-key="2525317e6f8b41509f0b08b99a681a4c:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="e119ac83ff9d494e9b3d74a52d42f57f"><span offset-key="e119ac83ff9d494e9b3d74a52d42f57f:0">Running any of these commands will create a directory called my-app inside the current folder. Inside that directory, it will generate the initial project structure and install the transitive dependencies:</span></span>

<span key="4d2c0fb6bf0a41e19c48a3d0b2790c56"><span offset-key="4d2c0fb6bf0a41e19c48a3d0b2790c56:0">No configuration or complicated folder structures, only the files you need to build your app. Once the installation is done, you can open your project folder:</span></span>

## 

<span key="0d76164d6708436981b303fc6ed98029"><span offset-key="0d76164d6708436981b303fc6ed98029:0">Scripts</span></span><a href="https://create-react-app.dev/docs/getting-started#scripts" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="2e5fa0e85ca84521a9443b5c06cbc133" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="9e6fad79cb914d488534eb76693c5e23"><span data-offset-key="9e6fad79cb914d488534eb76693c5e23:0">#</span></span></span></a><span key="29f9946d472c4e158f9538ec5e6f7eb4"><span offset-key="29f9946d472c4e158f9538ec5e6f7eb4:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="62aeb8c7901c4b1293de87761a628467"><span offset-key="62aeb8c7901c4b1293de87761a628467:0">Inside the newly created project, you can run some built-in commands:</span></span>

### 

<span key="a436c5b31143469ea95420e76cb70681"><span offset-key="a436c5b31143469ea95420e76cb70681:0">npm start or yarn start</span></span><a href="https://create-react-app.dev/docs/getting-started#npm-start-or-yarn-start" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="8754f502e32f444dbf8f1c52558d40ec" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="08ee99e072ea478f9965867678cbf14c"><span data-offset-key="08ee99e072ea478f9965867678cbf14c:0">#</span></span></span></a><span key="185f15a2d2ff4c0e95c7ef163f299fb8"><span offset-key="185f15a2d2ff4c0e95c7ef163f299fb8:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="730a7c859420453598642599a5191c20"><span offset-key="730a7c859420453598642599a5191c20:0">Runs the app in development mode. Open </span></span><a href="http://localhost:3000" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="13804b9619e243c786ae39d915b22269" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="d9f45fd8f2f64782ae0906f86dd2cfc3"><span data-offset-key="d9f45fd8f2f64782ae0906f86dd2cfc3:0">http://localhost:3000</span></span></span></a><span key="7e30b992094844969cfbf8b2296d40cd"><span offset-key="7e30b992094844969cfbf8b2296d40cd:0"> to view it in the browser.</span></span>

<span key="9872d12029904cbbac119c392b109bbc"><span offset-key="9872d12029904cbbac119c392b109bbc:0">The page will automatically reload if you make changes to the code. You will see the build errors and lint warnings in the console.</span></span>

### 

<span key="ffb3aa2e59124036b369acdc74110518"><span offset-key="ffb3aa2e59124036b369acdc74110518:0">npm test or yarn test</span></span><a href="https://create-react-app.dev/docs/getting-started#npm-test-or-yarn-test" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="fbf9da8ba960450a83be53a537572416" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="94dda5a1e9964b928cd3502469010e57"><span data-offset-key="94dda5a1e9964b928cd3502469010e57:0">#</span></span></span></a><span key="5b3009ceb62047ed9440fbb80cc90200"><span offset-key="5b3009ceb62047ed9440fbb80cc90200:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="1eb93f3137c947d699f1700befd0e7d5"><span offset-key="1eb93f3137c947d699f1700befd0e7d5:0">Runs the test watcher in an interactive mode. By default, runs tests related to files changed since the last commit.</span></span>

<span key="54a76e0468484979861168fe76492c12"><span offset-key="54a76e0468484979861168fe76492c12:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://create-react-app.dev/docs/running-tests" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="2c8e1ef0be4949be85b72f36dc631581" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="3a2207832bf44f2e82ed120135ad58f7"><span data-offset-key="3a2207832bf44f2e82ed120135ad58f7:0">Read more about testing</span></span></span></a><span key="eda5a75ba160418ba79c2e61e225438e"><span offset-key="eda5a75ba160418ba79c2e61e225438e:0">.</span></span>

### 

<span key="c91435f757f0420b89ada9e835960c68"><span offset-key="c91435f757f0420b89ada9e835960c68:0">npm run build or yarn build</span></span><a href="https://create-react-app.dev/docs/getting-started#npm-run-build-or-yarn-build" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="4e33896108544bebb8bba5f195e1de07" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="8a2acbc39e8e4ec7a60963bfd7830702"><span data-offset-key="8a2acbc39e8e4ec7a60963bfd7830702:0">#</span></span></span></a><span key="0e610fd5069945f29349f2fb3d9d598f"><span offset-key="0e610fd5069945f29349f2fb3d9d598f:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="8d56dad3ef4046788e31ee32c05b66c1"><span offset-key="8d56dad3ef4046788e31ee32c05b66c1:0">Builds the app for production to the build folder. It correctly bundles React in production mode and optimizes the build for the best performance.</span></span>

<span key="a3613ef6f6bf4b4f95a15b284de942cb"><span offset-key="a3613ef6f6bf4b4f95a15b284de942cb:0">The build is minified and the filenames include the hashes.</span></span>

<span key="54dbaeaaa164404db92950d78bb2ebd8"><span offset-key="54dbaeaaa164404db92950d78bb2ebd8:0">Your app is ready to be deployed.</span></span>

# 

<span key="d90061ca79a44c2a9e48914a5af0ce5c"><span offset-key="d90061ca79a44c2a9e48914a5af0ce5c:0">Folder Structuremy-app/ README.md node\_modules/ package.json public/ index.html favicon.ico src/ App.css App.js App.test.js index.css index.js logo.svg</span></span>

<span key="c196062cd06b493bacd910b5369b6e2e"><span offset-key="c196062cd06b493bacd910b5369b6e2e:0">After creation, your project should look like this:</span></span>

<span key="85aea372ac394bfca10fd5638ae5af77"><span offset-key="85aea372ac394bfca10fd5638ae5af77:0">For the project to build, </span>**these files must exist with exact filenames**<span offset-key="85aea372ac394bfca10fd5638ae5af77:2">:</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="51802ef916044c2eaa550e80689ef4e1"><span offset-key="51802ef916044c2eaa550e80689ef4e1:0">public/index.html is the page template;</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="f801f955dba54a26b3ea64512a431260"><span offset-key="f801f955dba54a26b3ea64512a431260:0">src/index.js is the JavaScript entry point.</span></span>

<span key="1123b7434d3945ca88823848f00af924"><span offset-key="1123b7434d3945ca88823848f00af924:0">You can delete or rename the other files.</span></span>

<span key="4fd9d5fe3d2c4014b9512d41192cb8e2"><span offset-key="4fd9d5fe3d2c4014b9512d41192cb8e2:0">You may create subdirectories inside src. For faster rebuilds, only files inside src are processed by webpack. You need to </span>**put any JS and CSS files inside src**<span offset-key="4fd9d5fe3d2c4014b9512d41192cb8e2:2">, otherwise webpack wonâ€™t see them.</span></span>

<span key="4bfc283d4bc0421d87b99a469f157989"><span offset-key="4bfc283d4bc0421d87b99a469f157989:0">Only files inside public can be used from public/index.html. Read instructions below for using assets from JavaScript and HTML.</span></span>

<span key="e0a4e25a330b4154917c2699d9070d75"><span offset-key="e0a4e25a330b4154917c2699d9070d75:0">You can, however, create more top-level directories. They will not be included in the production build so you can use them for things like documentation.</span></span>

<span key="79134305f5c4462ead0f9ec00c5b20b1"><span offset-key="79134305f5c4462ead0f9ec00c5b20b1:0">If you have Git installed and your project is not part of a larger repository, then a new repository will be initialized resulting in an additional top-level .git directory.</span></span>

# 

<span key="e3055fcfd2ff4b55b89dfd7405009850"><span offset-key="e3055fcfd2ff4b55b89dfd7405009850:0">Developing Components in Isolationnpx -p @storybook/cli sb initnpm install --save react-styleguidistyarn add react-styleguidist "scripts": {+ "styleguide": "styleguidist server",+ "styleguide:build": "styleguidist build", "start": "react-scripts start",npm run styleguide</span></span>

<span key="86b1493ff65740daacce70d8d788ce32"><span offset-key="86b1493ff65740daacce70d8d788ce32:0">Usually, in an app, you have a lot of UI components, and each of them has many different states. For an example, a basic button component could have the following states:</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="c4bb0f8ca96f4e7cadac90a6cccb6ba3"><span offset-key="c4bb0f8ca96f4e7cadac90a6cccb6ba3:0">In a regular state, with a text label.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="b7fc4206b82b4a7a938e69c591e0e9ae"><span offset-key="b7fc4206b82b4a7a938e69c591e0e9ae:0">In the disabled mode.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="2643af2a29f347beb3edd4239db8725d"><span offset-key="2643af2a29f347beb3edd4239db8725d:0">In a loading state.</span></span>

<span key="7d1ed9e4456e4f3f96d7a4298a921c73"><span offset-key="7d1ed9e4456e4f3f96d7a4298a921c73:0">Usually, itâ€™s hard to see these states without running a sample app or some examples.</span></span>

<span key="c92d62d96930429cb53d85753c0ed76a"><span offset-key="c92d62d96930429cb53d85753c0ed76a:0">Create React App doesnâ€™t include any tools for this by default, but you can add </span></span><a href="https://storybook.js.org" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="bfb038e9669c4929b12ecd30726dd18d" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="9b89b15c504c45b1ad1e6ffea56c8579"><span data-offset-key="9b89b15c504c45b1ad1e6ffea56c8579:0">Storybook for React</span></span></span></a><span key="5e8353b2138b4f359ebbf7bb4183d4c1"><span offset-key="5e8353b2138b4f359ebbf7bb4183d4c1:0"> (</span></span><a href="https://github.com/storybooks/storybook" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="b6107ff918c9487d85347d0c35c1f2a9" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="8f4fe9da153147489d3f0eecfd920c5b"><span data-offset-key="8f4fe9da153147489d3f0eecfd920c5b:0">source</span></span></span></a><span key="2991c3860e5a4bc0acf3e5289abf1e65"><span offset-key="2991c3860e5a4bc0acf3e5289abf1e65:0">) or </span></span><a href="https://react-styleguidist.js.org" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="42f891da4d844c198dd9bcb6d86d39db" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="3dad22c1aae24408afb0ff06dd5eae26"><span data-offset-key="3dad22c1aae24408afb0ff06dd5eae26:0">React Styleguidist</span></span></span></a><span key="e40794401f274658a866552357ea0124"><span offset-key="e40794401f274658a866552357ea0124:0"> (</span></span><a href="https://github.com/styleguidist/react-styleguidist" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="b568e95b1ab442e99eccd86b4039d26b" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="343a525751e140b18b8ac2a0349b0f4a"><span data-offset-key="343a525751e140b18b8ac2a0349b0f4a:0">source</span></span></span></a><span key="2af03bb0459840a5b5e03bcad9e3e0dc"><span offset-key="2af03bb0459840a5b5e03bcad9e3e0dc:0">) to your project. </span>**These are third-party tools that let you develop components and see all their states in isolation from your app**<span offset-key="2af03bb0459840a5b5e03bcad9e3e0dc:2">.</span></span>

<span key="7b2bf0d175ad454985f0ea749da4565f"><span offset-key="7b2bf0d175ad454985f0ea749da4565f:0">You can also deploy your Storybook or style guide as a static app. This way, everyone in your team can view and review different states of UI components without starting a backend server or creating an account in your app.</span></span>

## 

<span key="b8cbeae038214203b6f95a809b7818ef"><span offset-key="b8cbeae038214203b6f95a809b7818ef:0">Getting Started with Storybook</span></span><a href="https://create-react-app.dev/docs/developing-components-in-isolation#getting-started-with-storybook" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="ab97fbb64ee34cc3870bb509c873d44d" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="d82770b910c04f6bbbdd2312614c7b33"><span data-offset-key="d82770b910c04f6bbbdd2312614c7b33:0">#</span></span></span></a><span key="229e8540f34c4bc3ac376fc7030c5e44"><span offset-key="229e8540f34c4bc3ac376fc7030c5e44:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="edcf38567fc84148b2c6651565d9a0d6"><span offset-key="edcf38567fc84148b2c6651565d9a0d6:0">Storybook is a development environment for React UI components. It allows you to browse a component library, view the different states of each component, and interactively develop and test components.</span></span>

<span key="fc0ffbb32cf141d590d5d62b0646d952"><span offset-key="fc0ffbb32cf141d590d5d62b0646d952:0">Run the following command inside your appâ€™s directory:</span></span>

<span key="f976d1ba0f0f40799fe716ef9d20f6c2"><span offset-key="f976d1ba0f0f40799fe716ef9d20f6c2:0">After that, follow the instructions on the screen.</span></span>

<span key="2ddf041e7df54fb4abc4d10634a840ba"><span offset-key="2ddf041e7df54fb4abc4d10634a840ba:0">Learn more about React Storybook:</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="3660d6e2cfd1424d9f1262d5d55feac5"><span offset-key="3660d6e2cfd1424d9f1262d5d55feac5:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://learnstorybook.com" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="5e4f85ffa07048daaa062d22fe38f878" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="aed7c96280b44ba8b5b3b06109b0a2bd"><span data-offset-key="aed7c96280b44ba8b5b3b06109b0a2bd:0">Learn Storybook (tutorial)</span></span></span></a><span key="e993a7cd309847a0ba75bd6685dd860b"><span offset-key="e993a7cd309847a0ba75bd6685dd860b:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

## 

<span key="a7efcb021cad4d0891b9fcd5061c6c2b"><span offset-key="a7efcb021cad4d0891b9fcd5061c6c2b:0">Getting Started with Styleguidist</span></span><a href="https://create-react-app.dev/docs/developing-components-in-isolation#getting-started-with-styleguidist" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="2e05d5535f6d413bb46de9702ef4bbc7" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="fe0cc20e4e0a447981b0c9b8602fb3ed"><span data-offset-key="fe0cc20e4e0a447981b0c9b8602fb3ed:0">#</span></span></span></a><span key="915819f974e14e06b7fff827a7cea5ce"><span offset-key="915819f974e14e06b7fff827a7cea5ce:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="611696cd4b5f4b7997d120ce3c82dbab"><span offset-key="611696cd4b5f4b7997d120ce3c82dbab:0">Styleguidist combines a style guide, where all your components are presented on a single page with their props documentation and usage examples, with an environment for developing components in isolation, similar to Storybook. In Styleguidist you write examples in Markdown, where each code snippet is rendered as a live editable playground.</span></span>

<span key="e482a8a3bf5845d4995c46ecf79c659a"><span offset-key="e482a8a3bf5845d4995c46ecf79c659a:0">First, install Styleguidist:</span></span>

<span key="58b2e9303ee149b88996123bf02f341e"><span offset-key="58b2e9303ee149b88996123bf02f341e:0">Alternatively you may use yarn:</span></span>

<span key="c16c467de60f4ceb8d915b2b2c2366ea"><span offset-key="c16c467de60f4ceb8d915b2b2c2366ea:0">Then, add these scripts to your package.json:</span></span>

<span key="77e3e4e8b9b240688ecbef0cff37adf3"><span offset-key="77e3e4e8b9b240688ecbef0cff37adf3:0">Then, run the following command inside your appâ€™s directory:</span></span>

<span key="983daace5259423bbfb1fe2496c4e629"><span offset-key="983daace5259423bbfb1fe2496c4e629:0">After that, follow the instructions on the screen.</span></span>

<span key="780125bd69fa4233b265239323bcf2c9"><span offset-key="780125bd69fa4233b265239323bcf2c9:0">Learn more about React Styleguidist:</span></span>

    <span key="04386c863e28412cbd28a901886962ed"><span offset-key="04386c863e28412cbd28a901886962ed:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://github.com/styleguidist/react-styleguidist" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="3f426009f93c476290d00d403d3a1818" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="dc5f1b550a844940a4e8749a89547cfa"><span data-offset-key="dc5f1b550a844940a4e8749a89547cfa:0">GitHub Repo</span></span></span></a><span key="69a74297395f4078bd6f929317f16687"><span offset-key="69a74297395f4078bd6f929317f16687:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>
