# 

<span key="3f00eb6a7e5b4eecac6a9df8d2928a84"><span offset-key="3f00eb6a7e5b4eecac6a9df8d2928a84:0">Using HTTPS in Developmentset HTTPS=true&&npm start($env:HTTPS = "true") -and (npm start)HTTPS=true npm startHTTPS=true SSL\_CRT\_FILE=cert.crt SSL\_KEY\_FILE=cert.key npm startCopy{ "start": "HTTPS=true react-scripts start"}</span></span>

> <span key="e2b4b9a5891146aa9c498aae19b29a59"><span offset-key="e2b4b9a5891146aa9c498aae19b29a59:0">Note: this feature is available with </span></span><a href="../../../../../cdn-cgi/l/email-protection.html#cebcabafadbae3bdadbca7bebabd8efee0fae0fe" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="d8979bef04cc43afaebde25488f40a31" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="2763dbd8e8324db39f837be886933179"><span data-offset-key="2763dbd8e8324db39f837be886933179:0"><span class="__cf_email__" data-cfemail="394b5c585a4d144a5a4b50494d4a7909170d1709">[emailÂ protected]</span></span></span></span></a><span key="fc2a48fd48164b5b82ac46ab6b401c33"><span offset-key="fc2a48fd48164b5b82ac46ab6b401c33:0"> and higher.</span></span>

<span key="3ddc40fcb20943b3bef9110813436c9c"><span offset-key="3ddc40fcb20943b3bef9110813436c9c:0">You may require the dev server to serve pages over HTTPS. One particular case where this could be useful is when using </span></span><a href="https://create-react-app.dev/docs/proxying-api-requests-in-development" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="3a3fd13f719c4103a38702a5e832f391" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="fef6d823b2324bd5b65a6e0da7330e13"><span data-offset-key="fef6d823b2324bd5b65a6e0da7330e13:0">the "proxy" feature</span></span></span></a><span key="575467018eea45fab4a7a3785a44daf4"><span offset-key="575467018eea45fab4a7a3785a44daf4:0"> to proxy requests to an API server when that API server is itself serving HTTPS.</span></span>

<span key="14ecae7db43448bd80d0684a1f0f45d8"><span offset-key="14ecae7db43448bd80d0684a1f0f45d8:0">To do this, set the HTTPS environment variable to true, then start the dev server as usual with npm start:</span></span>

### 

<span key="aca4c23afda1436ab91b6fa4bc1bc180"><span offset-key="aca4c23afda1436ab91b6fa4bc1bc180:0">Windows (cmd.exe)</span></span><a href="https://create-react-app.dev/docs/using-https-in-development#windows-cmdexe" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="a22c31dd96cb4653976694d9e1d0e082" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="191a21c2bf4e455bb36a192c35382340"><span data-offset-key="191a21c2bf4e455bb36a192c35382340:0">#</span></span></span></a><span key="ea6246bcd2d143cc8db20ba4118f2da4"><span offset-key="ea6246bcd2d143cc8db20ba4118f2da4:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="ef46cf1eba38475a9d3fc2222f22b1f3"><span offset-key="ef46cf1eba38475a9d3fc2222f22b1f3:0">(Note: the lack of whitespace is intentional.)</span></span>

### 

<span key="7d49e7b35e4f43a199769ab139084308"><span offset-key="7d49e7b35e4f43a199769ab139084308:0">Windows (Powershell)</span></span><a href="https://create-react-app.dev/docs/using-https-in-development#windows-powershell" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="30e94bdc96e142ac9f8df2d965235467" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="11d5085fee524699b2fc965f3ae84740"><span data-offset-key="11d5085fee524699b2fc965f3ae84740:0">#</span></span></span></a><span key="c3085a838a58493d807d7e876a8029e1"><span offset-key="c3085a838a58493d807d7e876a8029e1:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

### 

<span key="9a15f314a19e49518d0247d55c8b2cc9"><span offset-key="9a15f314a19e49518d0247d55c8b2cc9:0">Linux, macOS (Bash)</span></span><a href="https://create-react-app.dev/docs/using-https-in-development#linux-macos-bash" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="8811c440e85a4ed2aa5e8166879fa1b3" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="75e64ac9805a488a84ddb0c1caff320d"><span data-offset-key="75e64ac9805a488a84ddb0c1caff320d:0">#</span></span></span></a><span key="e04567752c6e4da7b8d5f42594f789a5"><span offset-key="e04567752c6e4da7b8d5f42594f789a5:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="42650a7fea874bbab8d508e176b989ec"><span offset-key="42650a7fea874bbab8d508e176b989ec:0">Note that the server will use a self-signed certificate, so your web browser will almost definitely display a warning upon accessing the page.</span></span>

## 

<span key="b9fc4704054642d999bb6414d8281f48"><span offset-key="b9fc4704054642d999bb6414d8281f48:0">Custom SSL certificate</span></span><a href="https://create-react-app.dev/docs/using-https-in-development#custom-ssl-certificate" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="198b6fca220144b0ae980cd54531b1f1" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="2e6ab8f00b624e91ae2db09d2767c1e2"><span data-offset-key="2e6ab8f00b624e91ae2db09d2767c1e2:0">#</span></span></span></a><span key="b72ad4e16cf7438d9e11d7c20ec6fe7b"><span offset-key="b72ad4e16cf7438d9e11d7c20ec6fe7b:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="276c698f58b848bd8a1798c6f1b7f7c5"><span offset-key="276c698f58b848bd8a1798c6f1b7f7c5:0">To set a custom certificate, set the SSL\_CRT\_FILE and SSL\_KEY\_FILE environment variables to the path of the certificate and key files in the same way you do for HTTPS above. Note that you will also need to set HTTPS=true.</span></span>

### 

<span key="1fac3b12eb764f2eaa28bdd7c2f12f9c"><span offset-key="1fac3b12eb764f2eaa28bdd7c2f12f9c:0">Linux, macOS (Bash)</span></span><a href="https://create-react-app.dev/docs/using-https-in-development#linux-macos-bash-1" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="18988880386141a584f3870cf89b97c9" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="59176beade5d407f97fc6710c540a9e2"><span data-offset-key="59176beade5d407f97fc6710c540a9e2:0">#</span></span></span></a><span key="5d928ec1de844764a96d59db4e235cd0"><span offset-key="5d928ec1de844764a96d59db4e235cd0:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="8215897d278247b8b8b9e2ee5311a293"><span offset-key="8215897d278247b8b8b9e2ee5311a293:0">To avoid having to set the environment variable each time, you can either include in the npm start script like so:</span></span>

<span key="150dde4b42f544619c6ff4ee4878878d"><span offset-key="150dde4b42f544619c6ff4ee4878878d:0">Or you can create a .env file with HTTPS=true set. </span></span><a href="https://create-react-app.dev/docs/adding-custom-environment-variables" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="b7a4320d46fc450798f3b66ee6e2cdfe" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="00a7c7e9619748e5884b1a215def273b"><span data-offset-key="00a7c7e9619748e5884b1a215def273b:0">Learn more about environment variables in CRA</span></span></span></a><span key="dc90792f9ef344d3b81f375e8305191b"><span offset-key="dc90792f9ef344d3b81f375e8305191b:0">.</span></span>

# 

<span key="b182e5b31603414b872f9a28fb2b9f6d"><span offset-key="b182e5b31603414b872f9a28fb2b9f6d:0">Adding a Stylesheet.Button { padding: 20px;}</span>*import*<span offset-key="b182e5b31603414b872f9a28fb2b9f6d:2"> React, { Component } </span>*from*<span offset-key="b182e5b31603414b872f9a28fb2b9f6d:4"> 'react';</span>*import*<span offset-key="b182e5b31603414b872f9a28fb2b9f6d:6"> './Button.css'; </span>*// Tell webpack that Button.js uses these stylesclass*<span offset-key="b182e5b31603414b872f9a28fb2b9f6d:8"> Button </span>*extends*<span offset-key="b182e5b31603414b872f9a28fb2b9f6d:10"> Component { render() { </span>*// You can use them as regular CSS styles*<span offset-key="b182e5b31603414b872f9a28fb2b9f6d:12"> </span>*return*<span offset-key="b182e5b31603414b872f9a28fb2b9f6d:14"> &lt;div className="Button" />; }}</span></span>

<span key="c1dd38d5db824383a0418d13b20fa91a"><span offset-key="c1dd38d5db824383a0418d13b20fa91a:0">This project setup uses </span></span><a href="https://webpack.js.org" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="032d4d4966ff4eb9b61afcafc68fbc96" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="4cb26a4b206b49a79ae80ba340a46d57"><span data-offset-key="4cb26a4b206b49a79ae80ba340a46d57:0">webpack</span></span></span></a><span key="34f10bd8f42c44baa5c8dfa0300c8b41"><span offset-key="34f10bd8f42c44baa5c8dfa0300c8b41:0"> for handling all assets. webpack offers a custom way of â€œextendingâ€ the concept of import beyond JavaScript. To express that a JavaScript file depends on a CSS file, you need to </span>**import the CSS from the JavaScript file**<span offset-key="34f10bd8f42c44baa5c8dfa0300c8b41:2">:</span></span>

## 

<span key="f5c34ea59df3477f850b8bdea9c4e422"><span offset-key="f5c34ea59df3477f850b8bdea9c4e422:0">Button.css</span></span><a href="https://create-react-app.dev/docs/adding-a-stylesheet#buttoncss" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="b7a3a5d3aa3242348667b3dc8b84fd32" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="f263ac04cdc748c3b066ae42f300175f"><span data-offset-key="f263ac04cdc748c3b066ae42f300175f:0">#</span></span></span></a><span key="07cb311b76c548a9a5c5f30f9c61c84f"><span offset-key="07cb311b76c548a9a5c5f30f9c61c84f:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

## 

<span key="a0b8ccf7244a422d96bd556bbe0aa2dd"><span offset-key="a0b8ccf7244a422d96bd556bbe0aa2dd:0">Button.js</span></span><a href="https://create-react-app.dev/docs/adding-a-stylesheet#buttonjs" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="2491444e40864e33b6b9a85ec58537cd" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="6a43238222344bb782508793025de398"><span data-offset-key="6a43238222344bb782508793025de398:0">#</span></span></span></a><span key="75a0712b433942cc9190e4c61a548df7"><span offset-key="75a0712b433942cc9190e4c61a548df7:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="06e710dffbbf42a1a21644d1b4f3df0a">**This is not required for React**<span offset-key="06e710dffbbf42a1a21644d1b4f3df0a:1"> but many people find this feature convenient. You can read about the benefits of this approach </span></span><a href="https://medium.com/seek-blog/block-element-modifying-your-javascript-components-d7f99fcab52b" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="e89be0e3cf8c4a56aeaf364e946c2b62" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="d6f3a2779d1f4ef0a01b1233b14a0b43"><span data-offset-key="d6f3a2779d1f4ef0a01b1233b14a0b43:0">here</span></span></span></a><span key="bbcf591a5621414c9b04c919ddf3b38d"><span offset-key="bbcf591a5621414c9b04c919ddf3b38d:0">. However you should be aware that this makes your code less portable to other build tools and environments than webpack.</span></span>

<span key="cc0dc428a67248f78e53e80bfb45ba9a"><span offset-key="cc0dc428a67248f78e53e80bfb45ba9a:0">In development, expressing dependencies this way allows your styles to be reloaded on the fly as you edit them. In production, all CSS files will be concatenated into a single minified .css file in the build output.</span></span>

<span key="6e94c7042eaf4602b25500f68a7a7d15"><span offset-key="6e94c7042eaf4602b25500f68a7a7d15:0">If you are concerned about using webpack-specific semantics, you can put all your CSS right into src/index.css. It would still be imported from src/index.js, but you could always remove that import if you later migrate to a different build tool.</span></span>

# 

<span key="3aba1b2860804f769b4e46c4aa3bf331"><span offset-key="3aba1b2860804f769b4e46c4aa3bf331:0">Adding Images, Fonts, and Files\_import\_ React </span>*from*<span offset-key="3aba1b2860804f769b4e46c4aa3bf331:2"> 'react';</span>*import*<span offset-key="3aba1b2860804f769b4e46c4aa3bf331:4"> logo </span>*from*<span offset-key="3aba1b2860804f769b4e46c4aa3bf331:6"> './logo.png'; </span>*// Tell webpack this JS file uses this image\_console.log(logo);*<span offset-key="3aba1b2860804f769b4e46c4aa3bf331:8"> // /logo.84287d09.pngfunction </span>*Header() {*<span offset-key="3aba1b2860804f769b4e46c4aa3bf331:10"> // Import result is the URL of your image </span>*\_return*<span offset-key="3aba1b2860804f769b4e46c4aa3bf331:12"> &lt;img src={logo} alt="Logo" />;}</span>*export*<span offset-key="3aba1b2860804f769b4e46c4aa3bf331:14"> </span>*default*<span offset-key="3aba1b2860804f769b4e46c4aa3bf331:16"> Header;.Logo { background-image: url(./logo.png);}</span>*import*<span offset-key="3aba1b2860804f769b4e46c4aa3bf331:18"> { ReactComponent </span>*as*<span offset-key="3aba1b2860804f769b4e46c4aa3bf331:20"> Logo } </span>*from*<span offset-key="3aba1b2860804f769b4e46c4aa3bf331:22"> './logo.svg';</span>*function*<span offset-key="3aba1b2860804f769b4e46c4aa3bf331:24"> App() { </span>*return*<span offset-key="3aba1b2860804f769b4e46c4aa3bf331:26"> ( &lt;div> {</span>*/\* Logo is an actual React component \*/*<span offset-key="3aba1b2860804f769b4e46c4aa3bf331:28">} &lt;Logo /> &lt;/div> );}</span></span>

<span key="36d6ca101680440292272d715cb53c47"><span offset-key="36d6ca101680440292272d715cb53c47:0">With webpack, using static assets like images and fonts works similarly to CSS.</span></span>

<span key="329fa47d47ac4fc29acf136c2373cd6e"><span offset-key="329fa47d47ac4fc29acf136c2373cd6e:0">You can </span>**import a file right in a JavaScript module**<span offset-key="329fa47d47ac4fc29acf136c2373cd6e:2">. This tells webpack to include that file in the bundle. Unlike CSS imports, importing a file gives you a string value. This value is the final path you can reference in your code, e.g. as the src attribute of an image or the href of a link to a PDF.</span></span>

<span key="7781f15ade2d4da4a73889ce82708fce"><span offset-key="7781f15ade2d4da4a73889ce82708fce:0">To reduce the number of requests to the server, importing images that are less than 10,000 bytes returns a </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/HTTP/Basics_of_HTTP/Data_URIs" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="7ac30d103c6546fbb1c5abd23f25c444" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="8a06fa3ab1f24be69f1825ef8f64e2c5"><span data-offset-key="8a06fa3ab1f24be69f1825ef8f64e2c5:0">data URI</span></span></span></a><span key="5c7613eaa2774f41967c11ab999d99c0"><span offset-key="5c7613eaa2774f41967c11ab999d99c0:0"> instead of a path. This applies to the following file extensions: bmp, gif, jpg, jpeg, and png. SVG files are excluded due to </span></span><a href="https://github.com/facebook/create-react-app/issues/1153" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="a7f3ca4b58c448b58e4010e7c107552a" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="fb0faaa2013c4311ac3390fe0a8c52be"><span data-offset-key="fb0faaa2013c4311ac3390fe0a8c52be:0">#1153</span></span></span></a><span key="cdefc845dc38411bbe2faee3cd825cd9"><span offset-key="cdefc845dc38411bbe2faee3cd825cd9:0">. You can control the 10,000 byte threshold by setting the IMAGE\_INLINE\_SIZE\_LIMIT environment variable as documented in our </span></span><a href="https://create-react-app.dev/docs/advanced-configuration" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="c2faee00df1a4c409a907f1ee3603613" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="3632da1b03c24a19a002aa0de54056eb"><span data-offset-key="3632da1b03c24a19a002aa0de54056eb:0">advanced configuration</span></span></span></a><span key="e99a03650a0049b9925c785d5a49666a"><span offset-key="e99a03650a0049b9925c785d5a49666a:0">.</span></span>

<span key="9792a1fb8f754fc0a1001bd1afee6355"><span offset-key="9792a1fb8f754fc0a1001bd1afee6355:0">Here is an example:</span></span>

<span key="b6e8bef6856a42bdac8cf2699943275c"><span offset-key="b6e8bef6856a42bdac8cf2699943275c:0">This ensures that when the project is built, webpack will correctly move the images into the build folder, and provide us with correct paths.</span></span>

<span key="6e74fb5ab3d34785b55afd40e295b194"><span offset-key="6e74fb5ab3d34785b55afd40e295b194:0">This works in CSS too:</span></span>

<span key="4a0c1fd6e1d84265a6d18bb28a1933a7"><span offset-key="4a0c1fd6e1d84265a6d18bb28a1933a7:0">webpack finds all relative module references in CSS (they start with ./) and replaces them with the final paths from the compiled bundle. If you make a typo or accidentally delete an important file, you will see a compilation error, like when you import a non-existent JavaScript module. The final filenames in the compiled bundle are generated by webpack from content hashes. If the file content changes in the future, webpack will give it a different name in production so you donâ€™t need to worry about long-term caching of assets.</span></span>

<span key="b9eb3ff01d2d4dc396bc2a12fb30b5fd"><span offset-key="b9eb3ff01d2d4dc396bc2a12fb30b5fd:0">Please be advised that this is also a custom feature of webpack.</span></span>

<span key="e47bce9811274f0786b224bb1af81dae">**It is not required for React**<span offset-key="e47bce9811274f0786b224bb1af81dae:1"> but many people enjoy it (and React Native uses a similar mechanism for images).</span></span>

<span key="91f94e7affdc4bb48a470365292f5ae7"><span offset-key="91f94e7affdc4bb48a470365292f5ae7:0">An alternative way of handling static assets is described in the next section.</span></span>

## 

<span key="5ba2bd09764d4d03a03ec8af8eae2f5e"><span offset-key="5ba2bd09764d4d03a03ec8af8eae2f5e:0">Adding SVGs</span></span><a href="https://create-react-app.dev/docs/adding-images-fonts-and-files#adding-svgs" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="fda12bbb48b24178ae888ae1bc493432" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="3a42223086944db18c991d350dde792e"><span data-offset-key="3a42223086944db18c991d350dde792e:0">#</span></span></span></a><span key="9c816946d6f34b06a8171c595fda6fd5"><span offset-key="9c816946d6f34b06a8171c595fda6fd5:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

> <span key="f83fa5d7dfd64f0192e8d97310d78b17"><span offset-key="f83fa5d7dfd64f0192e8d97310d78b17:0">Note: this feature is available with </span></span><a href="../../../../../cdn-cgi/l/email-protection.html#1d6f787c7e69306e7e6f746d696e5d2f332d332d" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="30f9c39dbfec45c18142c7d0998af79c" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="d825db9a38b645f0bec570c631d0ce0c"><span data-offset-key="d825db9a38b645f0bec570c631d0ce0c:0"><span class="__cf_email__" data-cfemail="443621252730693727362d34303704766a746a74">[emailÂ protected]</span></span></span></span></a><span key="ac4ac4cc5f734c8bbc29c48d29767170"><span offset-key="ac4ac4cc5f734c8bbc29c48d29767170:0"> and higher, and </span></span><a href="../../../../../cdn-cgi/l/email-protection.html#6416010507102455524a574a54" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="3196d5945ebd4f2aa7d7fd58e0add03b" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-93055_259-93056-237__"><span data-key="2edd6ce1067c4b4ca009b807272fbe65"><span data-offset-key="2edd6ce1067c4b4ca009b807272fbe65:0"><span class="__cf_email__" data-cfemail="b2c0d7d3d1c6f283849c819c82">[emailÂ protected]</span></span></span></span></a><span key="58058b5ffbe848a784f3188dce4c6d03"><span offset-key="58058b5ffbe848a784f3188dce4c6d03:0"> and higher.</span></span>

<span key="5b6de87c93d244ec8664516f98387470"><span offset-key="5b6de87c93d244ec8664516f98387470:0">One way to add SVG files was described in the section above. You can also import SVGs directly as React components. You can use either of the two approaches. In your code it would look like this:</span></span>

<span key="420a5d5090dc48e69a493030c5fbcf31"><span offset-key="420a5d5090dc48e69a493030c5fbcf31:0">This is handy if you don't want to load SVG as a separate file. Don't forget the curly braces in the import! The ReactComponent import name is significant and tells Create React App that you want a React component that renders an SVG, rather than its filename.</span></span>

> <span key="d0fba8fb7d3d4d1aaee700943bc39775">**Tip:**<span offset-key="d0fba8fb7d3d4d1aaee700943bc39775:1"> The imported SVG React Component accepts a title prop along with other props that a svg element accepts. Use this prop to add an accessible title to your svg component.</span></span>

Lifting State Up

<a href="untitled.html#often-several-components-need-to-reflect-the-same-changing-data-we-recommend-lifting-the-shared-stat" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-855088 r-dwliz8 r-1loqt21 r-18u37iz r-lqms97 r-dnmrzs r-iphfwy r-1guathk r-1h8ys4a r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr r-7xmw5f"></a>

Often, several components need to reflect the same changing data. We recommend lifting the shared state up to their closest common ancestor. Let's see how this works in action.

<a href="untitled.html#adding-a-second-input" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-855088 r-dwliz8 r-1loqt21 r-18u37iz r-lqms97 r-dnmrzs r-iphfwy r-1guathk r-1h8ys4a r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr r-7xmw5f"></a>

Lessons Learned

<a href="untitled.html#composition-vs-inheritance" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-855088 r-dwliz8 r-1loqt21 r-18u37iz r-lqms97 r-dnmrzs r-iphfwy r-1guathk r-1h8ys4a r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr r-7xmw5f"></a>

Composition vs Inheritance

<a href="untitled.html#react-has-a-powerful-composition-model-and-we-recommend-using-composition-instead-of-inheritance-to" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-855088 r-dwliz8 r-1loqt21 r-18u37iz r-lqms97 r-dnmrzs r-iphfwy r-1guathk r-1h8ys4a r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr r-7xmw5f"></a>

React has a powerful composition model, and we recommend using composition instead of inheritance to reuse code between components.

<a href="untitled.html#containment" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-855088 r-dwliz8 r-1loqt21 r-18u37iz r-lqms97 r-dnmrzs r-iphfwy r-1guathk r-1h8ys4a r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr r-7xmw5f"></a>

Thinking in React

<a href="untitled.html#react-is-in-our-opinion-the-premier-way-to-build-big-fast-web-apps-with-javascript-it-has-scaled-ver" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-855088 r-dwliz8 r-1loqt21 r-18u37iz r-lqms97 r-dnmrzs r-iphfwy r-1guathk r-1h8ys4a r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr r-7xmw5f"></a>

React is, in our opinion, the premier way to build big, fast Web apps with JavaScript. It has scaled very well for us at Facebook and Instagram.
